\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l00720}00720 \textcolor{comment}{// On AddPolyline() and AddConvexPolyFilled() we intentionally avoid using ImVec2 and superfluous function calls to optimize debug/non-\/inlined builds.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l00721}00721 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Those macros expects l-\/values and need to be used as their own statement.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l00722}00722 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Those macros are intentionally not surrounded by the 'do \{\} while (0)' idiom because even that translates to runtime with debug compilers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l00723}00723 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_NORMALIZE2F\_OVER\_ZERO(VX,VY)     \{ float d2 = VX*VX + VY*VY; if (d2 > 0.0f) \{ float inv\_len = ImRsqrt(d2); VX *= inv\_len; VY *= inv\_len; \} \} (void)0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l00724}00724 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_FIXNORMAL2F\_MAX\_INVLEN2          100.0f }\textcolor{comment}{// 500.0f (see \#4053, \#3366)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l00725}00725 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_FIXNORMAL2F(VX,VY)               \{ float d2 = VX*VX + VY*VY; if (d2 > 0.000001f) \{ float inv\_len2 = 1.0f / d2; if (inv\_len2 > IM\_FIXNORMAL2F\_MAX\_INVLEN2) inv\_len2 = IM\_FIXNORMAL2F\_MAX\_INVLEN2; VX *= inv\_len2; VY *= inv\_len2; \} \} (void)0}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02410}02410         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dst\_tmp.GlyphsSet.Storage.empty())}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02411}02411             dst\_tmp.GlyphsSet.Create(dst\_tmp.GlyphsHighest + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02412}02412 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02413}02413         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keyword}{const} ImWchar* src\_range = src\_tmp.SrcRanges; src\_range[0] \&\& src\_range[1]; src\_range += 2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02414}02414             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} codepoint = src\_range[0]; codepoint <= src\_range[1]; codepoint++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02415}02415             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02416}02416                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dst\_tmp.GlyphsSet.TestBit(codepoint))    \textcolor{comment}{// Don't overwrite existing glyphs. We could make this an option for MergeMode (e.g. MergeOverwrite==true)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02417}02417                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{continue};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02418}02418                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbtt\_FindGlyphIndex(\&src\_tmp.FontInfo, codepoint))    \textcolor{comment}{// It is actually in the font?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02419}02419                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{continue};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02420}02420 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02421}02421                 \textcolor{comment}{// Add to avail set/counters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02422}02422                 src\_tmp.GlyphsCount++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02423}02423                 dst\_tmp.GlyphsCount++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02424}02424                 src\_tmp.GlyphsSet.SetBit(codepoint);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02425}02425                 dst\_tmp.GlyphsSet.SetBit(codepoint);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02426}02426                 total\_glyphs\_count++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02427}02427             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02428}02428     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02429}02429 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02430}02430     \textcolor{comment}{// 3. Unpack our bit map into a flat list (we now have all the Unicode points that we know are requested \_and\_ available \_and\_ not overlapping another)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02431}02431     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} src\_i = 0; src\_i < src\_tmp\_array.Size; src\_i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02432}02432     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02433}02433         \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_build_src_data}{ImFontBuildSrcData}}\& src\_tmp = src\_tmp\_array[src\_i];}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02435}02435         UnpackBitVectorToFlatIndexList(\&src\_tmp.GlyphsSet, \&src\_tmp.GlyphsList);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02436}02436         src\_tmp.GlyphsSet.Clear();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02437}02437         IM\_ASSERT(src\_tmp.GlyphsList.Size == src\_tmp.GlyphsCount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02438}02438     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02439}02439     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} dst\_i = 0; dst\_i < dst\_tmp\_array.Size; dst\_i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02440}02440         dst\_tmp\_array[dst\_i].GlyphsSet.Clear();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02441}02441     dst\_tmp\_array.clear();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02442}02442 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02443}02443     \textcolor{comment}{// Allocate packing character data and flag packed characters buffer as non-\/packed (x0=y0=x1=y1=0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02444}02444     \textcolor{comment}{// (We technically don't need to zero-\/clear buf\_rects, but let's do it for the sake of sanity)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02445}02445     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vector}{ImVector<stbrp\_rect>}} buf\_rects;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02446}02446     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vector}{ImVector<stbtt\_packedchar>}} buf\_packedchars;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02447}02447     buf\_rects.resize(total\_glyphs\_count);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02448}02448     buf\_packedchars.resize(total\_glyphs\_count);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02449}02449     memset(buf\_rects.Data, 0, (\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})buf\_rects.size\_in\_bytes());}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02450}02450     memset(buf\_packedchars.Data, 0, (\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})buf\_packedchars.size\_in\_bytes());}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02451}02451 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02452}02452     \textcolor{comment}{// 4. Gather glyphs sizes so we can pack them in our virtual canvas.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02453}02453     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} total\_surface = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02454}02454     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} buf\_rects\_out\_n = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02455}02455     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} buf\_packedchars\_out\_n = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02456}02456     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} src\_i = 0; src\_i < src\_tmp\_array.Size; src\_i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02457}02457     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02458}02458         \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_build_src_data}{ImFontBuildSrcData}}\& src\_tmp = src\_tmp\_array[src\_i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02459}02459         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (src\_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02460}02460             \textcolor{keywordflow}{continue};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02461}02461 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02462}02462         src\_tmp.Rects = \&buf\_rects[buf\_rects\_out\_n];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02463}02463         src\_tmp.PackedChars = \&buf\_packedchars[buf\_packedchars\_out\_n];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02464}02464         buf\_rects\_out\_n += src\_tmp.GlyphsCount;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02465}02465         buf\_packedchars\_out\_n += src\_tmp.GlyphsCount;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02466}02466 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02467}02467         \textcolor{comment}{// Convert our ranges in the format stb\_truetype wants}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02468}02468         \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_config}{ImFontConfig}}\& cfg = atlas-\/>ConfigData[src\_i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02469}02469         src\_tmp.PackRange.font\_size = cfg.SizePixels;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02470}02470         src\_tmp.PackRange.first\_unicode\_codepoint\_in\_range = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02471}02471         src\_tmp.PackRange.array\_of\_unicode\_codepoints = src\_tmp.GlyphsList.Data;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02472}02472         src\_tmp.PackRange.num\_chars = src\_tmp.GlyphsList.Size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02473}02473         src\_tmp.PackRange.chardata\_for\_range = src\_tmp.PackedChars;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02474}02474         src\_tmp.PackRange.h\_oversample = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)cfg.OversampleH;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02475}02475         src\_tmp.PackRange.v\_oversample = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char})cfg.OversampleV;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02476}02476 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02477}02477         \textcolor{comment}{// Gather the sizes of all rectangles we will need to pack (this loop is based on stbtt\_PackFontRangesGatherRects)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02478}02478         \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} scale = (cfg.SizePixels > 0) ? stbtt\_ScaleForPixelHeight(\&src\_tmp.FontInfo, cfg.SizePixels) : stbtt\_ScaleForMappingEmToPixels(\&src\_tmp.FontInfo, -\/cfg.SizePixels);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02479}02479         \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} padding = atlas-\/>TexGlyphPadding;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02480}02480         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} glyph\_i = 0; glyph\_i < src\_tmp.GlyphsList.Size; glyph\_i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02481}02481         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02482}02482             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x0, y0, x1, y1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02483}02483             \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} glyph\_index\_in\_font = stbtt\_FindGlyphIndex(\&src\_tmp.FontInfo, src\_tmp.GlyphsList[glyph\_i]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02484}02484             IM\_ASSERT(glyph\_index\_in\_font != 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02485}02485             stbtt\_GetGlyphBitmapBoxSubpixel(\&src\_tmp.FontInfo, glyph\_index\_in\_font, scale * cfg.OversampleH, scale * cfg.OversampleV, 0, 0, \&x0, \&y0, \&x1, \&y1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02486}02486             src\_tmp.Rects[glyph\_i].w = (stbrp\_coord)(x1 -\/ x0 + padding + cfg.OversampleH -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02487}02487             src\_tmp.Rects[glyph\_i].h = (stbrp\_coord)(y1 -\/ y0 + padding + cfg.OversampleV -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02488}02488             total\_surface += src\_tmp.Rects[glyph\_i].w * src\_tmp.Rects[glyph\_i].h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02489}02489         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02490}02490     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02491}02491 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02492}02492     \textcolor{comment}{// We need a width for the skyline algorithm, any width!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02493}02493     \textcolor{comment}{// The exact width doesn't really matter much, but some API/GPU have texture size limitations and increasing width can decrease height.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02494}02494     \textcolor{comment}{// User can override TexDesiredWidth and TexGlyphPadding if they wish, otherwise we use a simple heuristic to select the width based on expected surface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02495}02495     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} surface\_sqrt = (int)ImSqrt((\textcolor{keywordtype}{float})total\_surface) + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02496}02496     atlas-\/>TexHeight = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02497}02497     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (atlas-\/>TexDesiredWidth > 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02498}02498         atlas-\/>TexWidth = atlas-\/>TexDesiredWidth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02499}02499     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02500}02500         atlas-\/>TexWidth = (surface\_sqrt >= 4096 * 0.7f) ? 4096 : (surface\_sqrt >= 2048 * 0.7f) ? 2048 : (surface\_sqrt >= 1024 * 0.7f) ? 1024 : 512;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02501}02501 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02502}02502     \textcolor{comment}{// 5. Start packing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02503}02503     \textcolor{comment}{// Pack our extra data rectangles first, so it will be on the upper-\/left corner of our texture (UV will have small values).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02504}02504     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} TEX\_HEIGHT\_MAX = 1024 * 32;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02505}02505     \mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt__pack__context}{stbtt\_pack\_context}} spc = \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02506}02506     stbtt\_PackBegin(\&spc, NULL, atlas-\/>TexWidth, TEX\_HEIGHT\_MAX, 0, atlas-\/>TexGlyphPadding, NULL);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02507}02507     ImFontAtlasBuildPackCustomRects(atlas, spc.pack\_info);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02508}02508 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02509}02509     \textcolor{comment}{// 6. Pack each source font. No rendering yet, we are working with rectangles in an infinitely tall texture at this point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02510}02510     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} src\_i = 0; src\_i < src\_tmp\_array.Size; src\_i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02511}02511     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02512}02512         \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_build_src_data}{ImFontBuildSrcData}}\& src\_tmp = src\_tmp\_array[src\_i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02513}02513         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (src\_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02514}02514             \textcolor{keywordflow}{continue};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02515}02515 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02516}02516         stbrp\_pack\_rects((\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbrp__context}{stbrp\_context}}*)spc.pack\_info, src\_tmp.Rects, src\_tmp.GlyphsCount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02517}02517 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02518}02518         \textcolor{comment}{// Extend texture height and mark missing glyphs as non-\/packed so we won't render them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02519}02519         \textcolor{comment}{// FIXME: We are not handling packing failure here (would happen if we got off TEX\_HEIGHT\_MAX or if a single if larger than TexWidth?)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02520}02520         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} glyph\_i = 0; glyph\_i < src\_tmp.GlyphsCount; glyph\_i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02521}02521             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (src\_tmp.Rects[glyph\_i].was\_packed)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02522}02522                 atlas-\/>TexHeight = ImMax(atlas-\/>TexHeight, src\_tmp.Rects[glyph\_i].y + src\_tmp.Rects[glyph\_i].h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02523}02523     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02524}02524 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02525}02525     \textcolor{comment}{// 7. Allocate texture}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02526}02526     atlas-\/>TexHeight = (atlas-\/>Flags \& ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoPowerOfTwoHeight) ? (atlas-\/>TexHeight + 1) : ImUpperPowerOfTwo(atlas-\/>TexHeight);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02527}02527     atlas-\/>TexUvScale = \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}(1.0f / atlas-\/>TexWidth, 1.0f / atlas-\/>TexHeight);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02528}02528     atlas-\/>TexPixelsAlpha8 = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)IM\_ALLOC(atlas-\/>TexWidth * atlas-\/>TexHeight);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02529}02529     memset(atlas-\/>TexPixelsAlpha8, 0, atlas-\/>TexWidth * atlas-\/>TexHeight);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02530}02530     spc.pixels = atlas-\/>TexPixelsAlpha8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02531}02531     spc.height = atlas-\/>TexHeight;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02532}02532 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02533}02533     \textcolor{comment}{// 8. Render/rasterize font characters into the texture}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02534}02534     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} src\_i = 0; src\_i < src\_tmp\_array.Size; src\_i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02535}02535     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02536}02536         \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_config}{ImFontConfig}}\& cfg = atlas-\/>ConfigData[src\_i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02537}02537         \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_build_src_data}{ImFontBuildSrcData}}\& src\_tmp = src\_tmp\_array[src\_i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02538}02538         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (src\_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02540}02540 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02541}02541         stbtt\_PackFontRangesRenderIntoRects(\&spc, \&src\_tmp.FontInfo, \&src\_tmp.PackRange, 1, src\_tmp.Rects);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02542}02542 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02543}02543         \textcolor{comment}{// Apply multiply operator}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02544}02544         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (cfg.RasterizerMultiply != 1.0f)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02545}02545         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02546}02546             \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} multiply\_table[256];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02547}02547             ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyCalcLookupTable(multiply\_table, cfg.RasterizerMultiply);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02548}02548             \mbox{\hyperlink{structstbrp__rect}{stbrp\_rect}}* r = \&src\_tmp.Rects[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02549}02549             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} glyph\_i = 0; glyph\_i < src\_tmp.GlyphsCount; glyph\_i++, r++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02550}02550                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r-\/>was\_packed)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02551}02551                     ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyRectAlpha8(multiply\_table, atlas-\/>TexPixelsAlpha8, r-\/>x, r-\/>y, r-\/>w, r-\/>h, atlas-\/>TexWidth * 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02552}02552         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02553}02553         src\_tmp.Rects = NULL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02554}02554     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02555}02555 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02556}02556     \textcolor{comment}{// End packing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02557}02557     stbtt\_PackEnd(\&spc);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02558}02558     buf\_rects.clear();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02559}02559 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02560}02560     \textcolor{comment}{// 9. Setup ImFont and glyphs for runtime}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02561}02561     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} src\_i = 0; src\_i < src\_tmp\_array.Size; src\_i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02562}02562     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02563}02563         \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_build_src_data}{ImFontBuildSrcData}}\& src\_tmp = src\_tmp\_array[src\_i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02564}02564         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (src\_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02565}02565             \textcolor{keywordflow}{continue};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02566}02566 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02567}02567         \textcolor{comment}{// When merging fonts with MergeMode=true:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__draw_8cpp_source_l02568}02568         \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ We can have multiple input fonts writing into a same destination font.}}
